< Text>
I‚Äôve been training at Gracie Barra in Irvine for approximately a year and a half.  Before I started training here, I had never done any type of formal martial arts training so walking into the academy on the first day was very intimidating.  On top of my lack of experience with martial arts, I was also in fairly bad shape from a few years in grad school and work.

What I was hoping to get out of training at Gracie Barra was to find an activity that was physically and mentally challenging and something that I would stay with.  I had started and stopped my membership at the gym numerous times and I just found it was too boring and I never pushed myself hard enough.

So in January of 2016 I signed up for a free class and the process was very easy and the ladies at the counter were so friendly that it made it less intimidating.  I signed up right after the intro class and it‚Äôs been everything I was looking for.

What I love most about training at Gracie Barra are the world-class instructors (Professors) that truly care about their students and also a plethora of great training partners that make this sport so enjoyable.  There‚Äôs truly a fellowship all the members of Gracie Barra and sense of caring for the people we are training with.

I would recommend anyone looking to learn self-defense and stay in shape to first train Brazilian Jiu Jitsu and second to train at Gracie Barra.  The last year and a half have exceeded my expectations and I‚Äôve even put my kids as well.  (The kids classes are fantastic)

Thanks to Professors and Staff at Gracie Barra for providing such an excellent school and life changing experience for my family and I.</Text>

<Time>1465010312754< /Time><Rate>5</Rate><review>Gracie Barra HQ in Irvine has a progressive kids and adult (men, women and mix) program.  The culture of the school, for the most part, is welcoming to new students.  Higher belts try to help the lower belts through the drills.  In addition, the culture is very family-centric with many parents and kids that compete in local and world tournaments.  The instructors are very technical and provide a pragmatic approach to sport, mma and self-defense.  Any day of the week you will see a numerous higher level belts, including many black belts during the adult classes.  The head instructor, Professor Philipe Della Monica, has an extensive list of fighters that he trains (present and past UFC champions).  His expertise is apparent as he models basic and variations to techniques for different levels within the class.  You will be hard pressed to find a well rounded BJJ school.<//review>< Pics>

I have so many great things to say about Gracie Barra Irvine that I honestly don't know where to begin. I will start by saying that this is a world class facility with world class instructors in terms of Brazilian Jiu-Jitsu. I have been practicing "the gentle art" on and off through out the past 16 years and have had the opportunity to view & participate at different gyms/facilities. I have yet to come across a BJJ academy that is as diverse and well rounded as Gracie Barra Irvine.

Head instructor professor Philipe De La Monica has the academy running like a well oiled machine. The curriculum that he provides caters to many body types, level of athleticism, and age groups. The academy also caters to those that are interested in the sport for competition as well as those who are interested in the sport for other reasons (fitness, self defense, etc.). What I like most about Gracie Barra Irvine is the friendly atmosphere and lack of ego's. I have been to gyms where the sole focus is sport jiu-jitsu and many sparing partners have malicious intent. It is rare that this happens at Gracie Barra Irvine, there is a certain level of respect for each other as well as consideration for the safety/well being of training partners.

If you have been on the fence about trying Brazilian Jiu-Jitsu, I urge you to not waste another minute and come try a class at Gracie Barra Irvine. You won't be disappointed.< /Review>

<Rate>5<//Rate>< Review>
I've been training here since 2009 and have had a great experience. The Gracie Barra motto is "Jiu-Jitsu for Everyone" and there is something for everyone here. I strongly encourage you to come by the academy and see for yourself, but if you need the information:

BEGINNERS / CASUAL BJJ PRACTITIONERS: If you're just starting, they always make you feel welcome here. Some of the best people I've ever met are from here at Gracie Barra HQ.

SERIOUS COMPETITORS: If you're a serious competitor, there is never a shortage of talent. In the advanced and black belt classes, there are so many tough training partners. Even during the lunch time classes, there are a lot of brown and purple belts to test yourself.

KIDS: Brearin is one of the best in the business when it comes to teaching the kids. He has a lot of energy and knows how to have fun, but he is good at keeping he kids focused on learning. Coach Rod is also awesome with the kids too. The curriculum itself is not just BJJ centric and teaches kids different life lessons as well.

WOMEN: Women are always welcome in the regular classes, but they also have a women's program that is geared towards different aspects of BJJ.

TRAVELERS: When you sign up at one Gracie Barra, you can go to any of them worldwide. That way, you have no excuse not to train! There are a lot in the SoCal area alone and it's also a good way to make sure you train with other people you're not familiar with and don't get too familiar with the same people.

OTHER NOTES:

Over the years, there have been so many great instructors. More recently, Professor Philipe Della Monica has taken over as the head instructor and has continued to grow ever since. He is very well respected in the BJJ and MMA community as a competitor and coach. He is super friendly, but what stands out is his passion for teaching and his professionalism. He runs the school meticulously and even when he travels to teach seminars or corner MMA fighters, he is always back as soon as possible to teach. We are lucky to have him.

The point is that they're always working to improve the BJJ experience for you and you can't ask for anything more out of a BJJ school or any organization for that matter.< /Review>

<Text>I'll start by admitting that I've only started training here very recently, so these are more of my initial impressions. I'll probably provide an updated review in a few months.

The tagline for the GB franchise is "Jiu-Jitsu for Everyone", and that describes the atmosphere at GB Headquarters perfectly in that it is excellent at accommodating people with different goals for learning BJJ. Some people are doing it for fitness, others for self defense (like me), others for competition and MMA training, and so on. The students are also of all different shapes, sizes, and levels of athleticism as well.   Regardless of those factors, all of them are meeting their goals through learning the art of BJJ. The instructors have a base of expertise that is diverse enough to answer questions and tailor their teaching to accommodate these different perspectives and aims.

Everyone I've come across is friendly and willing to help, and I have not encountered any egos in the other students as of this writing. The instructors are also patient at breaking down moves and principles, answering questions, and teaching at a pace where beginners like myself can pick it up. Great atmosphere for a beginner like me - who is small, not very flexible, fairly uncoordinated, and pretty out of shape.

I've had classes with about 5 different instructors so far. The curriculum each week is standardized, so the techniques/principles that are taught are the same but each instructor has a slightly different teaching style where they emphasize different points about the same set of moves. I personally like this, as it allows a student to learn a technique not only by its steps, but by its principles and options for when and when not to apply them.

A final positive is that they don't have long-term contracts like other gyms, so if something happens such that you're unable to train, you won't be locked in. That was a deciding factor for me signing up here, since I'm a student.

In short, I highly recommend it so far, especially to beginners regardless of their goals or level of athleticism.

Check back in a few months for an update.</Text>< pics>
None< /pics>

Solid food at a great quality:quantity:price point, especially for lunch specials ($8-10).  Service was friendly and attentive. Don't go here for decor--it's in a space adjacent to a supermarket.  I think comparable to Sam Woo (which might be a tad better) but they take credit cards (unlike cash-only Sam Woo), it's not as crazy busy, and thus service seem less gruff. This place is in a grocery store.  The dim sum su Mai was fresh, but lacked flavor.
The baked charsui bao was  soft, freshly made and delicious but was short on filling. Chicken feet was flavorful but semi tough.  The beef chow funny was excellent perfect blend of soyu, beef, sprouts, ginger, sugar and fun rice noodles. I was visiting the area. And this place was the closest.
I would venture to say there may be other options, but in a pinch this would suffice. Pricing is moderate. Aloha< /Text>

<Review>It's an average looking food court kind of kiosk inside of a grocery store. However, they do make some nice dim sum and some excellent rice porridge, both of which exceeded expectations.

We got siu mai (pork and shrimp), har gao (shrimp dumplings), xiao lum bao (soup dumplings), baked BBQ bao, Magic Rice Wrapped (sticky rice with chicken), and egg rolls. The egg rolls were average, but everything else ranged from very good to excellent. The pork porridge with preserved eggs in particular is really well done, very well seasoned, and the pork in it is so tender It's hard to believe. We will definitely be back for more!<//Review>< pictures>

< username>
teadrinkerxyz<//username>
<time>1580186046118</time><Rating>4< /Rating>< text>
Came here to buy some roasted pork for the Lunar NewYear.  We ended upp with 2+ pounds of roast pork, 1/2 of a chicken, and 2 orders of fa gao (a light sponge cake).

Service:  good.   Server was nice to tell me  about the choicess of chicken.  Knowing that I was buying food to  celebrate the lunar new year, she told  me about a celebration in the  nearby public library.  Was smiling all the time when we  carried a conversation.

Food:  surprisingly good quality!!! The skin of the roasted pork was crispy.   The meat  was seasoned with the right amount of salt and spices.  Each piece was cut perfectly and assembled nicely in the box, see picture.   I sometimes get my roasted pork  from a store in Clairemont Mesa.   This place has  better  service and quality!  The sponge cake has good texture and not so sweet.

Like this place and will visit again for bbq takeouts.</text>
